         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         import os
         
         DATA_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), 'data')
         
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_current_weather():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'current_weather.txt')
             current_weather = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         cw = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_name': parts[1],
                             'temperature': int(parts[2]),
                             'condition': parts[3],
                             'humidity': int(parts[4]),
                             'wind_speed': int(parts[5]),
                             'last_updated': parts[6]
                         }
                         current_weather.append(cw)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return current_weather
         
         
         def load_forecasts():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'forecasts.txt')
             forecasts = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         fc = {
                             'forecast_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'high_temp': int(parts[3]),
                             'low_temp': int(parts[4]),
                             'condition': parts[5],
                             'precipitation': int(parts[6]),
                             'humidity': int(parts[7])
                         }
                         forecasts.append(fc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return forecasts
         
         
         def load_locations():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'locations.txt')
             locations = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         loc = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_name': parts[1],
                             'latitude': float(parts[2]),
                             'longitude': float(parts[3]),
                             'country': parts[4],
                             'timezone': parts[5]
                         }
                         locations.append(loc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return locations
         
         
         def load_alerts():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'alerts.txt')
             alerts = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         alert = {
                             'alert_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'alert_type': parts[2],
                             'severity': parts[3],
                             'description': parts[4],
                             'start_time': parts[5],
                             'end_time': parts[6],
                             'is_acknowledged': bool(int(parts[7]))
                         }
                         alerts.append(alert)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return alerts
         
         
         def load_air_quality():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'air_quality.txt')
             air_quality = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         aqi = {
                             'aqi_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'aqi_index': int(parts[2]),
                             'pm25': float(parts[3]),
                             'pm10': float(parts[4]),
                             'no2': float(parts[5]),
                             'o3': float(parts[6]),
                             'last_updated': parts[7]
                         }
                         air_quality.append(aqi)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return air_quality
         
         
         def load_saved_locations():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'saved_locations.txt')
             saved_locations = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         sloc = {
                             'saved_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'user_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'location_name': parts[3],
                             'is_default': int(parts[4])
                         }
                         saved_locations.append(sloc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return saved_locations
         
         
         # Helper for getting default location from saved_locations
         # If no saved location or none default, fallback to first current_weather record or None
         
         def get_default_location():
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             # Filter saved_locations of user_id 1 (assumed fixed user)
             user_saved = [loc for loc in saved_locations if loc['user_id'] == 1]
             default_saved = next((loc for loc in user_saved if loc['is_default'] == 1), None)
             if default_saved:
                 # Find full current weather data for this location id
                 all_current = load_current_weather()
                 for cw in all_current:
                     if cw['location_id'] == default_saved['location_id']:
                         # assemble dict per spec for dashboard
                         return {
                             'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                             'location_name': cw['location_name'],
                             'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                             'condition': cw['condition'],
                             'humidity': cw['humidity'],
                             'wind_speed': cw['wind_speed'],
                             'last_updated': cw['last_updated']
                         }
             # fallback
             current_list = load_current_weather()
             if current_list:
                 first = current_list[0]
                 return {
                     'location_id': first['location_id'],
                     'location_name': first['location_name'],
                     'temperature': first['temperature'],
                     'condition': first['condition'],
                     'humidity': first['humidity'],
                     'wind_speed': first['wind_speed'],
                     'last_updated': first['last_updated']
                 }
             return None
         
         
         # Flask Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             default_location = get_default_location() or {
                 'location_id': 0,
                 'location_name': 'Unknown',
                 'temperature': 0,
                 'condition': 'Unknown',
                 'humidity': 0,
                 'wind_speed': 0,
                 'last_updated': ''
             }
             return render_template('dashboard.html', default_location=default_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/weather/current/<int:location_id>')
         def current_weather(location_id):
             current_data = load_current_weather()
             # find location weather
             location_weather = next((cw for cw in current_data if cw['location_id'] == location_id), None)
             # get location basic info
             location_info = None
             all_locations = load_locations()
             for loc in all_locations:
                 if loc['location_id'] == location_id:
                     location_info = {'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']}
                     break
             if location_weather is None or location_info is None:
                 # fallback return with unknowns
                 location_info = location_info or {'location_id': location_id, 'location_name': 'Unknown'}
                 return render_template('current_weather.html', location=location_info, temperature=0, condition='Unknown', humidity=0, wind_speed=0)
         
             return render_template('current_weather.html',
                                    location=location_info,
                                    temperature=location_weather['temperature'],
                                    condition=location_weather['condition'],
                                    humidity=location_weather['humidity'],
                                    wind_speed=location_weather['wind_speed'])
         
         
         @app.route('/forecast/weekly')
         def weekly_forecast():
             locations = load_locations()
             forecasts = load_forecasts()
         
             selected_location_id = request.args.get('location_id', type=int)
         
             if selected_location_id is None and locations:
                 selected_location_id = locations[0]['location_id']
         
             # filter forecasts by selected location
             filtered_forecasts = [f for f in forecasts if f['location_id'] == selected_location_id] if selected_location_id is not None else []
         
             return render_template('weekly_forecast.html',
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    selected_location_id=selected_location_id or 0,
                                    forecasts=filtered_forecasts)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/search', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def location_search():
             locations = load_locations()
             saved_locations_all = load_saved_locations()
         
             # Filter saved locations for user_id 1 (fixed user)
             saved_locations = [
                 {'location_id': sloc['location_id'], 'location_name': sloc['location_name']}
                 for sloc in saved_locations_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1
             ]
         
             search_query = ''
             search_results = []
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     # Case insensitive search on location_name in locations data
                     search_results = [
                         loc for loc in locations if search_query.lower() in loc['location_name'].lower()
                     ]
             return render_template('location_search.html',
                                    search_query=search_query,
                                    search_results=search_results,
                                    saved_locations=saved_locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/alerts')
         def alerts():
             severity_filter = request.args.get('severity', 'All')
             location_filter_raw = request.args.get('location')
         
             try:
                 location_filter = int(location_filter_raw) if location_filter_raw is not None else None
             except ValueError:
                 location_filter = None
         
             alerts_all = load_alerts()
             locations_all = load_locations()
         
             # Filter alerts by severity and location
             def alert_severity_filter(alert):
                 if severity_filter == 'All':
                     return True
                 return alert['severity'] == severity_filter
         
             def alert_location_filter(alert):
                 if location_filter is None:
                     return True
                 return alert['location_id'] == location_filter
         
             filtered_alerts = [alert for alert in alerts_all if alert_severity_filter(alert) and alert_location_filter(alert)]
         
             # Prepare locations list for filter dropdown
             locations = [{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations_all]
         
             return render_template('alerts.html',
                                    alerts=filtered_alerts,
                                    severity_filter=severity_filter,
                                    location_filter=location_filter,
                                    locations=locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/air_quality')
         def air_quality():
             locations = load_locations()
         
             selected_location_id = request.args.get('location_id', type=int)
             if selected_location_id is None and locations:
                 selected_location_id = locations[0]['location_id']
         
             air_quality_list = load_air_quality()
             air_quality_data = next((a for a in air_quality_list if a['location_id'] == selected_location_id), None)
         
             aqi_description = ''
             health_recommendation = ''
         
             if air_quality_data:
                 aqi_val = air_quality_data['aqi_index']
                 # Determine AQI description and health recommendation based on AQI index
                 if aqi_val <= 50:
                     aqi_description = 'Good'
                     health_recommendation = 'Air quality is satisfactory. No health implications.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 100:
                     aqi_description = 'Moderate'
                     health_recommendation = 'Air quality is acceptable. Some pollutants may be a moderate health concern.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 150:
                     aqi_description = 'Unhealthy for Sensitive Groups'
                     health_recommendation = 'People with respiratory or heart disease should limit prolonged exertion.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 200:
                     aqi_description = 'Unhealthy'
                     health_recommendation = 'Everyone may begin to experience health effects; sensitive groups may experience more serious effects.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 300:
                     aqi_description = 'Very Unhealthy'
                     health_recommendation = 'Health alert: everyone may experience more serious health effects.'
                 else:
                     aqi_description = 'Hazardous'
                     health_recommendation = 'Health warnings of emergency conditions. Everyone should avoid outdoor exertion.'
         
             else:
                 # default empty
                 air_quality_data = {
                     'aqi_index': 0,
                     'pm25': 0.0,
                     'pm10': 0.0,
                     'no2': 0.0,
                     'o3': 0.0,
                     'last_updated': ''
                 }
         
             return render_template('air_quality.html',
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    selected_location_id=selected_location_id or 0,
                                    air_quality=air_quality_data,
                                    aqi_description=aqi_description,
                                    health_recommendation=health_recommendation)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/saved')
         def saved_locations():
             saved_locs_all = load_saved_locations()
             # Filter by user_id = 1 (fixed user)
             user_saved = [sloc for sloc in saved_locs_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1]
         
             current_weather_list = load_current_weather()
         
             # Build list with temperature and condition from current_weather for each saved location
             locations_detail = []
             for sloc in user_saved:
                 cw = next((cw for cw in current_weather_list if cw['location_id'] == sloc['location_id']), None)
                 if cw:
                     loc_dict = {
                         'location_id': sloc['location_id'],
                         'location_name': sloc['location_name'],
                         'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                         'condition': cw['condition']
                     }
                     locations_detail.append(loc_dict)
                 else:
                     locations_detail.append({
                         'location_id': sloc['location_id'],
                         'location_name': sloc['location_name'],
                         'temperature': 0,
                         'condition': 'Unknown'
                     })
         
             return render_template('saved_locations.html', locations=locations_detail)
         
         
         @app.route('/settings', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def settings():
             temperature_units = ['Celsius', 'Fahrenheit', 'Kelvin']
             locations = load_locations()
             saved_locations_all = load_saved_locations()
             user_saved = [sloc for sloc in saved_locations_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1]
         
             # Default settings placeholders
             # In absence of persistent user settings storage, store settings in server-side globals or defaults
             # For now, simulate we have defaults and get from query or form
         
             # We'll use Flask session or global dictionary to simulate settings storage for the app runtime
             from flask import session
             if 'current_unit' not in session:
                 session['current_unit'] = 'Celsius'
             if 'default_location_id' not in session:
                 # Determine default location id from saved locations
                 default_loc = next((loc for loc in user_saved if loc['is_default'] == 1), None)
                 session['default_location_id'] = default_loc['location_id'] if default_loc else (user_saved[0]['location_id'] if user_saved else 0)
             if 'alert_notifications_enabled' not in session:
                 session['alert_notifications_enabled'] = True
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 unit = request.form.get('temperature_unit')
                 def_loc_id_str = request.form.get('default_location_id')
                 alert_notify_raw = request.form.get('alert_notifications_enabled')
         
                 if unit in temperature_units:
                     session['current_unit'] = unit
         
                 try:
                     def_loc_id = int(def_loc_id_str)
                     # Check if this location exists in saved locations
                     if any(loc['location_id'] == def_loc_id for loc in user_saved):
                         session['default_location_id'] = def_loc_id
                 except (ValueError, TypeError):
                     pass
         
                 session['alert_notifications_enabled'] = bool(alert_notify_raw == 'on')
         
                 return redirect(url_for('settings'))
         
             return render_template('settings.html',
                                    temperature_units=temperature_units,
                                    current_unit=session.get('current_unit', 'Celsius'),
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    default_location_id=session.get('default_location_id', 0),
                                    alert_notifications_enabled=session.get('alert_notifications_enabled', True))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
         <meta charset="UTF-8">
         <title>Weather Dashboard</title>
         </head>
         <body>
         <div id="dashboard-page">
           <div id="current-weather-summary">
             <h2>Current Weather Summary</h2>
             <p>Location: {{ default_location.location_name }}</p>
             <p>Temperature: {{ default_location.temperature }}&deg;C</p>
             <p>Condition: {{ default_location.condition }}</p>
             <p>Humidity: {{ default_location.humidity }}%</p>
             <p>Wind Speed: {{ default_location.wind_speed }} mph</p>
             <p>Last Updated: {{ default_location.last_updated }}</p>
           </div>

         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         import os
         
         DATA_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), 'data')
         
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_current_weather():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'current_weather.txt')
             current_weather = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         cw = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_name': parts[1],
                             'temperature': int(parts[2]),
                             'condition': parts[3],
                             'humidity': int(parts[4]),
                             'wind_speed': int(parts[5]),
                             'last_updated': parts[6]
                         }
                         current_weather.append(cw)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return current_weather
         
         
         def load_forecasts():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'forecasts.txt')
             forecasts = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         fc = {
                             'forecast_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'high_temp': int(parts[3]),
                             'low_temp': int(parts[4]),
                             'condition': parts[5],
                             'precipitation': int(parts[6]),
                             'humidity': int(parts[7])
                         }
                         forecasts.append(fc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return forecasts
         
         
         def load_locations():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'locations.txt')
             locations = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         loc = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_name': parts[1],
                             'latitude': float(parts[2]),
                             'longitude': float(parts[3]),
                             'country': parts[4],
                             'timezone': parts[5]
                         }
                         locations.append(loc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return locations
         
         
         def load_alerts():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'alerts.txt')
             alerts = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         alert = {
                             'alert_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'alert_type': parts[2],
                             'severity': parts[3],
                             'description': parts[4],
                             'start_time': parts[5],
                             'end_time': parts[6],
                             'is_acknowledged': bool(int(parts[7]))
                         }
                         alerts.append(alert)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return alerts
         
         
         def load_air_quality():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'air_quality.txt')
             air_quality = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         aqi = {
                             'aqi_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'aqi_index': int(parts[2]),
                             'pm25': float(parts[3]),
                             'pm10': float(parts[4]),
                             'no2': float(parts[5]),
                             'o3': float(parts[6]),
                             'last_updated': parts[7]
                         }
                         air_quality.append(aqi)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return air_quality
         
         
         def load_saved_locations():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'saved_locations.txt')
             saved_locations = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         sloc = {
                             'saved_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'user_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'location_name': parts[3],
                             'is_default': int(parts[4])
                         }
                         saved_locations.append(sloc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return saved_locations
         
         
         # Helper for getting default location from saved_locations
         # If no saved location or none default, fallback to first current_weather record or None
         
         def get_default_location():
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             # Filter saved_locations of user_id 1 (assumed fixed user)
             user_saved = [loc for loc in saved_locations if loc['user_id'] == 1]
             default_saved = next((loc for loc in user_saved if loc['is_default'] == 1), None)
             if default_saved:
                 # Find full current weather data for this location id
                 all_current = load_current_weather()
                 for cw in all_current:
                     if cw['location_id'] == default_saved['location_id']:
                         # assemble dict per spec for dashboard
                         return {
                             'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                             'location_name': cw['location_name'],
                             'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                             'condition': cw['condition'],
                             'humidity': cw['humidity'],
                             'wind_speed': cw['wind_speed'],
                             'last_updated': cw['last_updated']
                         }
             # fallback
             current_list = load_current_weather()
             if current_list:
                 first = current_list[0]
                 return {
                     'location_id': first['location_id'],
                     'location_name': first['location_name'],
                     'temperature': first['temperature'],
                     'condition': first['condition'],
                     'humidity': first['humidity'],
                     'wind_speed': first['wind_speed'],
                     'last_updated': first['last_updated']
                 }
             return None
         
         
         # Flask Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             default_location = get_default_location() or {
                 'location_id': 0,
                 'location_name': 'Unknown',
                 'temperature': 0,
                 'condition': 'Unknown',
                 'humidity': 0,
                 'wind_speed': 0,
                 'last_updated': ''
             }
             return render_template('dashboard.html', default_location=default_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/weather/current/<int:location_id>')
         def current_weather(location_id):
             current_data = load_current_weather()
             # find location weather
             location_weather = next((cw for cw in current_data if cw['location_id'] == location_id), None)
             # get location basic info
             location_info = None
             all_locations = load_locations()
             for loc in all_locations:
                 if loc['location_id'] == location_id:
                     location_info = {'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']}
                     break
             if location_weather is None or location_info is None:
                 # fallback return with unknowns
                 location_info = location_info or {'location_id': location_id, 'location_name': 'Unknown'}
                 return render_template('current_weather.html', location=location_info, temperature=0, condition='Unknown', humidity=0, wind_speed=0)
         
             return render_template('current_weather.html',
                                    location=location_info,
                                    temperature=location_weather['temperature'],
                                    condition=location_weather['condition'],
                                    humidity=location_weather['humidity'],
                                    wind_speed=location_weather['wind_speed'])
         
         
         @app.route('/forecast/weekly')
         def weekly_forecast():
             locations = load_locations()
             forecasts = load_forecasts()
         
             selected_location_id = request.args.get('location_id', type=int)
         
             if selected_location_id is None and locations:
                 selected_location_id = locations[0]['location_id']
         
             # filter forecasts by selected location
             filtered_forecasts = [f for f in forecasts if f['location_id'] == selected_location_id] if selected_location_id is not None else []
         
             return render_template('weekly_forecast.html',
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    selected_location_id=selected_location_id or 0,
                                    forecasts=filtered_forecasts)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/search', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def location_search():
             locations = load_locations()
             saved_locations_all = load_saved_locations()
         
             # Filter saved locations for user_id 1 (fixed user)
             saved_locations = [
                 {'location_id': sloc['location_id'], 'location_name': sloc['location_name']}
                 for sloc in saved_locations_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1
             ]
         
             search_query = ''
             search_results = []
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     # Case insensitive search on location_name in locations data
                     search_results = [
                         loc for loc in locations if search_query.lower() in loc['location_name'].lower()
                     ]
             return render_template('location_search.html',
                                    search_query=search_query,
                                    search_results=search_results,
                                    saved_locations=saved_locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/alerts')
         def alerts():
             severity_filter = request.args.get('severity', 'All')
             location_filter_raw = request.args.get('location')
         
             try:
                 location_filter = int(location_filter_raw) if location_filter_raw is not None else None
             except ValueError:
                 location_filter = None
         
             alerts_all = load_alerts()
             locations_all = load_locations()
         
             # Filter alerts by severity and location
             def alert_severity_filter(alert):
                 if severity_filter == 'All':
                     return True
                 return alert['severity'] == severity_filter
         
             def alert_location_filter(alert):
                 if location_filter is None:
                     return True
                 return alert['location_id'] == location_filter
         
             filtered_alerts = [alert for alert in alerts_all if alert_severity_filter(alert) and alert_location_filter(alert)]
         
             # Prepare locations list for filter dropdown
             locations = [{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations_all]
         
             return render_template('alerts.html',
                                    alerts=filtered_alerts,
                                    severity_filter=severity_filter,
                                    location_filter=location_filter,
                                    locations=locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/air_quality')
         def air_quality():
             locations = load_locations()
         
             selected_location_id = request.args.get('location_id', type=int)
             if selected_location_id is None and locations:
                 selected_location_id = locations[0]['location_id']
         
             air_quality_list = load_air_quality()
             air_quality_data = next((a for a in air_quality_list if a['location_id'] == selected_location_id), None)
         
             aqi_description = ''
             health_recommendation = ''
         
             if air_quality_data:
                 aqi_val = air_quality_data['aqi_index']
                 # Determine AQI description and health recommendation based on AQI index
                 if aqi_val <= 50:
                     aqi_description = 'Good'
                     health_recommendation = 'Air quality is satisfactory. No health implications.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 100:
                     aqi_description = 'Moderate'
                     health_recommendation = 'Air quality is acceptable. Some pollutants may be a moderate health concern.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 150:
                     aqi_description = 'Unhealthy for Sensitive Groups'
                     health_recommendation = 'People with respiratory or heart disease should limit prolonged exertion.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 200:
                     aqi_description = 'Unhealthy'
                     health_recommendation = 'Everyone may begin to experience health effects; sensitive groups may experience more serious effects.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 300:
                     aqi_description = 'Very Unhealthy'
                     health_recommendation = 'Health alert: everyone may experience more serious health effects.'
                 else:
                     aqi_description = 'Hazardous'
                     health_recommendation = 'Health warnings of emergency conditions. Everyone should avoid outdoor exertion.'
         
             else:
                 # default empty
                 air_quality_data = {
                     'aqi_index': 0,
                     'pm25': 0.0,
                     'pm10': 0.0,
                     'no2': 0.0,
                     'o3': 0.0,
                     'last_updated': ''
                 }
         
             return render_template('air_quality.html',
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    selected_location_id=selected_location_id or 0,
                                    air_quality=air_quality_data,
                                    aqi_description=aqi_description,
                                    health_recommendation=health_recommendation)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/saved')
         def saved_locations():
             saved_locs_all = load_saved_locations()
             # Filter by user_id = 1 (fixed user)
             user_saved = [sloc for sloc in saved_locs_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1]
         
             current_weather_list = load_current_weather()
         
             # Build list with temperature and condition from current_weather for each saved location
             locations_detail = []
             for sloc in user_saved:
                 cw = next((cw for cw in current_weather_list if cw['location_id'] == sloc['location_id']), None)
                 if cw:
                     loc_dict = {
                         'location_id': sloc['location_id'],
                         'location_name': sloc['location_name'],
                         'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                         'condition': cw['condition']
                     }
                     locations_detail.append(loc_dict)
                 else:
                     locations_detail.append({
                         'location_id': sloc['location_id'],
                         'location_name': sloc['location_name'],
                         'temperature': 0,
                         'condition': 'Unknown'
                     })
         
             return render_template('saved_locations.html', locations=locations_detail)
         
         
         @app.route('/settings', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def settings():
             temperature_units = ['Celsius', 'Fahrenheit', 'Kelvin']
             locations = load_locations()
             saved_locations_all = load_saved_locations()
             user_saved = [sloc for sloc in saved_locations_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1]
         
             # Default settings placeholders
             # In absence of persistent user settings storage, store settings in server-side globals or defaults
             # For now, simulate we have defaults and get from query or form
         
             # We'll use Flask session or global dictionary to simulate settings storage for the app runtime
             from flask import session
             if 'current_unit' not in session:
                 session['current_unit'] = 'Celsius'
             if 'default_location_id' not in session:
                 # Determine default location id from saved locations
                 default_loc = next((loc for loc in user_saved if loc['is_default'] == 1), None)
                 session['default_location_id'] = default_loc['location_id'] if default_loc else (user_saved[0]['location_id'] if user_saved else 0)
             if 'alert_notifications_enabled' not in session:
                 session['alert_notifications_enabled'] = True
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 unit = request.form.get('temperature_unit')
                 def_loc_id_str = request.form.get('default_location_id')
                 alert_notify_raw = request.form.get('alert_notifications_enabled')
         
                 if unit in temperature_units:
                     session['current_unit'] = unit
         
                 try:
                     def_loc_id = int(def_loc_id_str)
                     # Check if this location exists in saved locations
                     if any(loc['location_id'] == def_loc_id for loc in user_saved):
                         session['default_location_id'] = def_loc_id
                 except (ValueError, TypeError):
                     pass
         
                 session['alert_notifications_enabled'] = bool(alert_notify_raw == 'on')
         
                 return redirect(url_for('settings'))
         
             return render_template('settings.html',
                                    temperature_units=temperature_units,
                                    current_unit=session.get('current_unit', 'Celsius'),
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    default_location_id=session.get('default_location_id', 0),
                                    alert_notifications_enabled=session.get('alert_notifications_enabled', True))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         import os
         
         DATA_DIR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), 'data')
         
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def load_current_weather():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'current_weather.txt')
             current_weather = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         cw = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_name': parts[1],
                             'temperature': int(parts[2]),
                             'condition': parts[3],
                             'humidity': int(parts[4]),
                             'wind_speed': int(parts[5]),
                             'last_updated': parts[6]
                         }
                         current_weather.append(cw)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return current_weather
         
         
         def load_forecasts():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'forecasts.txt')
             forecasts = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         fc = {
                             'forecast_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'high_temp': int(parts[3]),
                             'low_temp': int(parts[4]),
                             'condition': parts[5],
                             'precipitation': int(parts[6]),
                             'humidity': int(parts[7])
                         }
                         forecasts.append(fc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return forecasts
         
         
         def load_locations():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'locations.txt')
             locations = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         loc = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_name': parts[1],
                             'latitude': float(parts[2]),
                             'longitude': float(parts[3]),
                             'country': parts[4],
                             'timezone': parts[5]
                         }
                         locations.append(loc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return locations
         
         
         def load_alerts():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'alerts.txt')
             alerts = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         alert = {
                             'alert_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'alert_type': parts[2],
                             'severity': parts[3],
                             'description': parts[4],
                             'start_time': parts[5],
                             'end_time': parts[6],
                             'is_acknowledged': bool(int(parts[7]))
                         }
                         alerts.append(alert)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return alerts
         
         
         def load_air_quality():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'air_quality.txt')
             air_quality = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         aqi = {
                             'aqi_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'aqi_index': int(parts[2]),
                             'pm25': float(parts[3]),
                             'pm10': float(parts[4]),
                             'no2': float(parts[5]),
                             'o3': float(parts[6]),
                             'last_updated': parts[7]
                         }
                         air_quality.append(aqi)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return air_quality
         
         
         def load_saved_locations():
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'saved_locations.txt')
             saved_locations = []
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as file:
                     for line in file:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         sloc = {
                             'saved_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'user_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'location_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'location_name': parts[3],
                             'is_default': int(parts[4])
                         }
                         saved_locations.append(sloc)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return saved_locations
         
         
         # Helper for getting default location from saved_locations
         # If no saved location or none default, fallback to first current_weather record or None
         
         def get_default_location():
             saved_locations = load_saved_locations()
             # Filter saved_locations of user_id 1 (assumed fixed user)
             user_saved = [loc for loc in saved_locations if loc['user_id'] == 1]
             default_saved = next((loc for loc in user_saved if loc['is_default'] == 1), None)
             if default_saved:
                 # Find full current weather data for this location id
                 all_current = load_current_weather()
                 for cw in all_current:
                     if cw['location_id'] == default_saved['location_id']:
                         # assemble dict per spec for dashboard
                         return {
                             'location_id': cw['location_id'],
                             'location_name': cw['location_name'],
                             'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                             'condition': cw['condition'],
                             'humidity': cw['humidity'],
                             'wind_speed': cw['wind_speed'],
                             'last_updated': cw['last_updated']
                         }
             # fallback
             current_list = load_current_weather()
             if current_list:
                 first = current_list[0]
                 return {
                     'location_id': first['location_id'],
                     'location_name': first['location_name'],
                     'temperature': first['temperature'],
                     'condition': first['condition'],
                     'humidity': first['humidity'],
                     'wind_speed': first['wind_speed'],
                     'last_updated': first['last_updated']
                 }
             return None
         
         
         # Flask Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             default_location = get_default_location() or {
                 'location_id': 0,
                 'location_name': 'Unknown',
                 'temperature': 0,
                 'condition': 'Unknown',
                 'humidity': 0,
                 'wind_speed': 0,
                 'last_updated': ''
             }
             return render_template('dashboard.html', default_location=default_location)
         
         
         @app.route('/weather/current/<int:location_id>')
         def current_weather(location_id):
             current_data = load_current_weather()
             # find location weather
             location_weather = next((cw for cw in current_data if cw['location_id'] == location_id), None)
             # get location basic info
             location_info = None
             all_locations = load_locations()
             for loc in all_locations:
                 if loc['location_id'] == location_id:
                     location_info = {'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']}
                     break
             if location_weather is None or location_info is None:
                 # fallback return with unknowns
                 location_info = location_info or {'location_id': location_id, 'location_name': 'Unknown'}
                 return render_template('current_weather.html', location=location_info, temperature=0, condition='Unknown', humidity=0, wind_speed=0)
         
             return render_template('current_weather.html',
                                    location=location_info,
                                    temperature=location_weather['temperature'],
                                    condition=location_weather['condition'],
                                    humidity=location_weather['humidity'],
                                    wind_speed=location_weather['wind_speed'])
         
         
         @app.route('/forecast/weekly')
         def weekly_forecast():
             locations = load_locations()
             forecasts = load_forecasts()
         
             selected_location_id = request.args.get('location_id', type=int)
         
             if selected_location_id is None and locations:
                 selected_location_id = locations[0]['location_id']
         
             # filter forecasts by selected location
             filtered_forecasts = [f for f in forecasts if f['location_id'] == selected_location_id] if selected_location_id is not None else []
         
             return render_template('weekly_forecast.html',
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    selected_location_id=selected_location_id or 0,
                                    forecasts=filtered_forecasts)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/search', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def location_search():
             locations = load_locations()
             saved_locations_all = load_saved_locations()
         
             # Filter saved locations for user_id 1 (fixed user)
             saved_locations = [
                 {'location_id': sloc['location_id'], 'location_name': sloc['location_name']}
                 for sloc in saved_locations_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1
             ]
         
             search_query = ''
             search_results = []
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     # Case insensitive search on location_name in locations data
                     search_results = [
                         loc for loc in locations if search_query.lower() in loc['location_name'].lower()
                     ]
             return render_template('location_search.html',
                                    search_query=search_query,
                                    search_results=search_results,
                                    saved_locations=saved_locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/alerts')
         def alerts():
             severity_filter = request.args.get('severity', 'All')
             location_filter_raw = request.args.get('location')
         
             try:
                 location_filter = int(location_filter_raw) if location_filter_raw is not None else None
             except ValueError:
                 location_filter = None
         
             alerts_all = load_alerts()
             locations_all = load_locations()
         
             # Filter alerts by severity and location
             def alert_severity_filter(alert):
                 if severity_filter == 'All':
                     return True
                 return alert['severity'] == severity_filter
         
             def alert_location_filter(alert):
                 if location_filter is None:
                     return True
                 return alert['location_id'] == location_filter
         
             filtered_alerts = [alert for alert in alerts_all if alert_severity_filter(alert) and alert_location_filter(alert)]
         
             # Prepare locations list for filter dropdown
             locations = [{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations_all]
         
             return render_template('alerts.html',
                                    alerts=filtered_alerts,
                                    severity_filter=severity_filter,
                                    location_filter=location_filter,
                                    locations=locations)
         
         
         @app.route('/air_quality')
         def air_quality():
             locations = load_locations()
         
             selected_location_id = request.args.get('location_id', type=int)
             if selected_location_id is None and locations:
                 selected_location_id = locations[0]['location_id']
         
             air_quality_list = load_air_quality()
             air_quality_data = next((a for a in air_quality_list if a['location_id'] == selected_location_id), None)
         
             aqi_description = ''
             health_recommendation = ''
         
             if air_quality_data:
                 aqi_val = air_quality_data['aqi_index']
                 # Determine AQI description and health recommendation based on AQI index
                 if aqi_val <= 50:
                     aqi_description = 'Good'
                     health_recommendation = 'Air quality is satisfactory. No health implications.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 100:
                     aqi_description = 'Moderate'
                     health_recommendation = 'Air quality is acceptable. Some pollutants may be a moderate health concern.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 150:
                     aqi_description = 'Unhealthy for Sensitive Groups'
                     health_recommendation = 'People with respiratory or heart disease should limit prolonged exertion.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 200:
                     aqi_description = 'Unhealthy'
                     health_recommendation = 'Everyone may begin to experience health effects; sensitive groups may experience more serious effects.'
                 elif aqi_val <= 300:
                     aqi_description = 'Very Unhealthy'
                     health_recommendation = 'Health alert: everyone may experience more serious health effects.'
                 else:
                     aqi_description = 'Hazardous'
                     health_recommendation = 'Health warnings of emergency conditions. Everyone should avoid outdoor exertion.'
         
             else:
                 # default empty
                 air_quality_data = {
                     'aqi_index': 0,
                     'pm25': 0.0,
                     'pm10': 0.0,
                     'no2': 0.0,
                     'o3': 0.0,
                     'last_updated': ''
                 }
         
             return render_template('air_quality.html',
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    selected_location_id=selected_location_id or 0,
                                    air_quality=air_quality_data,
                                    aqi_description=aqi_description,
                                    health_recommendation=health_recommendation)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations/saved')
         def saved_locations():
             saved_locs_all = load_saved_locations()
             # Filter by user_id = 1 (fixed user)
             user_saved = [sloc for sloc in saved_locs_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1]
         
             current_weather_list = load_current_weather()
         
             # Build list with temperature and condition from current_weather for each saved location
             locations_detail = []
             for sloc in user_saved:
                 cw = next((cw for cw in current_weather_list if cw['location_id'] == sloc['location_id']), None)
                 if cw:
                     loc_dict = {
                         'location_id': sloc['location_id'],
                         'location_name': sloc['location_name'],
                         'temperature': cw['temperature'],
                         'condition': cw['condition']
                     }
                     locations_detail.append(loc_dict)
                 else:
                     locations_detail.append({
                         'location_id': sloc['location_id'],
                         'location_name': sloc['location_name'],
                         'temperature': 0,
                         'condition': 'Unknown'
                     })
         
             return render_template('saved_locations.html', locations=locations_detail)
         
         
         @app.route('/settings', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def settings():
             temperature_units = ['Celsius', 'Fahrenheit', 'Kelvin']
             locations = load_locations()
             saved_locations_all = load_saved_locations()
             user_saved = [sloc for sloc in saved_locations_all if sloc['user_id'] == 1]
         
             # Default settings placeholders
             # In absence of persistent user settings storage, store settings in server-side globals or defaults
             # For now, simulate we have defaults and get from query or form
         
             # We'll use Flask session or global dictionary to simulate settings storage for the app runtime
             from flask import session
             if 'current_unit' not in session:
                 session['current_unit'] = 'Celsius'
             if 'default_location_id' not in session:
                 # Determine default location id from saved locations
                 default_loc = next((loc for loc in user_saved if loc['is_default'] == 1), None)
                 session['default_location_id'] = default_loc['location_id'] if default_loc else (user_saved[0]['location_id'] if user_saved else 0)
             if 'alert_notifications_enabled' not in session:
                 session['alert_notifications_enabled'] = True
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 unit = request.form.get('temperature_unit')
                 def_loc_id_str = request.form.get('default_location_id')
                 alert_notify_raw = request.form.get('alert_notifications_enabled')
         
                 if unit in temperature_units:
                     session['current_unit'] = unit
         
                 try:
                     def_loc_id = int(def_loc_id_str)
                     # Check if this location exists in saved locations
                     if any(loc['location_id'] == def_loc_id for loc in user_saved):
                         session['default_location_id'] = def_loc_id
                 except (ValueError, TypeError):
                     pass
         
                 session['alert_notifications_enabled'] = bool(alert_notify_raw == 'on')
         
                 return redirect(url_for('settings'))
         
             return render_template('settings.html',
                                    temperature_units=temperature_units,
                                    current_unit=session.get('current_unit', 'Celsius'),
                                    locations=[{'location_id': loc['location_id'], 'location_name': loc['location_name']} for loc in locations],
                                    default_location_id=session.get('default_location_id', 0),
                                    alert_notifications_enabled=session.get('alert_notifications_enabled', True))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
         <meta charset="UTF-8">
         <title>Settings</title>
         </head>
         <body>
         <div id="settings-page">
             <h1>Settings</h1>
             <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('settings') }}">
                 <label for="temperature-unit-select">Temperature Unit:</label>
                 <select id="temperature-unit-select" name="temperature_unit">
                     {% for unit in temperature_units %}
                         <option value="{{ unit }}" {% if unit == current_unit %}selected{% endif %}>{{ unit }}</option>
                     {% endfor %}
